class="b17vyawb" href="/news/cat/tw_quo">台股盤勢</a></div></section><article class="mfxje1x"><section class="t1el8oye"><span class="bzubwch"> <!-- -->台股</span><h1>〈台股開盤〉挑戰歷史高點28554點台積電打退堂鼓 拖累大盤翻小黑</h1></section><p class="alr4vq1"><span class="signature">鉅亨網記者劉玟妤 台股</span><span class="separator"></span><time dateTime="2025-12-09T01:56:38.000Z">2025-12-09 09:56</time></p><main id="article-container" class="c1tt5pk2" style="--c1tt5pk2-0:20px"><section style="margin-top:30px"><p>美國聯準會即將召開年底最後一次政策會議，市場觀望氣氛濃厚，美股四大指數大多走弱，台股今 (9) 日在連漲 5 天後，挑戰歷史高點 28554 點乏力，早盤以 28364.04 點開高，最高漲至 28390.24 點，距離歷史高點只差 164 點，不過盤中台積電翻黑，拖累大盤小跌至 28211.06 點，預估成交量 5700 億元。</p></section><p><template id="P:1"></template></p><section style="margin-top:30px">

</section><section style="margin-top:30px"><p>觀察電子權值股今天表現，台積電 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/2330" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:2330:STOCK:COMMON">2330-TW</a>) 早盤以 1495 元開平盤後，一度重回 1500 元，不過隨後翻黑 1490 元，約跌 0.33%，聯發科 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/2454" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:2454:STOCK:COMMON">2454-TW</a>) 跌 0.35%，台達電 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/2308" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:2308:STOCK:COMMON">2308-TW</a>) 跌 0.82%。另外，鴻海 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/2317" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:2317:STOCK:COMMON">2317-TW</a>) 漲 0.65%，廣達 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/2382" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:2382:STOCK:COMMON">2382-TW</a>) 漲 0.34%，日月光 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/3711" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:3711:STOCK:COMMON">3711-TW</a>) 漲 0.21%。&nbsp;</p></section><section>

</section><div id="div-gpt-ad-cnyes_news_article_middle_1" class="a1mzdm1v" style="--a1mzdm1v-0:728px;--a1mzdm1v-1:90px;--a1mzdm1v-2:728px;--a1mzdm1v-3:90px;--a1mzdm1v-4:32px;--a1mzdm1v-5:32px;--a1mzdm1v-6:auto;--a1mzdm1v-7:auto"><span aria-live="polite" aria-busy="true"><span class="react-loading-skeleton" style="border-radius:6px;width:100%;height:100%">‌</span><br/></span></div><section style="margin-top:30px"><p>台塑四寶昨 (8) 日公告 11 月營收，呈現「一好三淡」，使得台塑四寶今天表現弱勢，台塑 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/1301" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:1301:STOCK:COMMON">1301-TW</a>)、台化 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/1326" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:1326:STOCK:COMMON">1326-TW</a>)、南亞 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/1303" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:1303:STOCK:COMMON">1303-TW</a>) 皆跌逾 3%，而台塑化 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/6505" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:6505:STOCK:COMMON">6505-TW</a>) 為唯一 11 月成長的公司，跌幅相對小，跌逾 1%。&nbsp;</p></section><section style="margin-top:30px">
